Prompt str:  // Assume that you have two 8-bit 2's complement numbers, a[7:0] and b[7:0]. These numbers are added to produce s[7:0]. Also compute whether a (signed) overflow has occurred.
// Hint: A signed overflow occurs when adding two positive numbers produces a negative result, or adding two negative numbers produces a positive result. There are several methods to detect overflow: It could be computed by comparing the signs of the input and output numbers, or derived from the carry-out of bit n and n-1.
// Finish the implementation of this module below.

    input [7:0] a,
    input [7:0] b,
    output [7:0] s,
    output overflow
);

// Assume that you have two 8-bit 2's complement numbers, a[7:0] and b[7:0]. These numbers are added to produce s[7:0]. Also compute whether a (signed) overflow has occurred.
// Hint: A signed overflow occurs when adding two positive numbers produces a negative result, or adding two negative numbers produces a positive result. There are several methods to detect overflow: It could be computed by comparing the signs of the input and output numbers, or derived from the carry-out of bit n and n-1.
// Finish the implementation of this module below.
module signedaddition (
    input [7:0] a,
    input [7:0] b,
    output [7:0] s,
    output overflow
);
    wire [7:0] sum;
    wire carry;
    
    fulladder_1bit fa0 (a[0], b[0], 1'b0, sum[0], carry);
    fulladder_1bit fa1 (a[1], b[1], carry, sum[1], carry);
    fulladder_1bit fa2 (a[2], b[2], carry, sum[2], carry);
    fulladder_1bit fa3 (a[3], b[3], carry, sum[3], carry);
    fulladder_1bit fa4 (a[4], b[4], carry, sum[4], carry);
    fulladder_1bit fa5 (a[5], b[5], carry, sum[5], carry);
    fulladder_1bit fa6 (a[6], b[6], carry, sum[6], carry);
    fulladder_1bit fa7 (a[7], b[7], carry, sum[7], carry);
    
    assign s = sum;
    assign overflow = carry;
endmodule
